<h2 id="examples" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#examples"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Examples</h2>
<h3 id="basic" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#basic"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Basic</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Here&#x27;s a basic example of the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Steps</code> component.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_4fhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_4fhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_4fhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="controlled" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#controlled"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Controlled</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Using the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">RootProvider</code> component, you can control the active step by using the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">step</code> prop and handling the
<code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">onStepChange</code> event.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_4lhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_4lhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_4lhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="root-provider" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#root-provider"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Root Provider</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">An alternative way to control the steps is to use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">RootProvider</code> component and the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">useSteps</code> hook. This way you can
access the state and methods from outside the component.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_4rhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_4rhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_4rhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="vertical" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#vertical"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Vertical</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">orientation</code> prop to display the steps vertically.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_51hanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_51hanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_51hanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h2 id="api-reference" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#api-reference"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>API Reference</h2>
<h3 id="props" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#props"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Props</h3>

Anatomy\n\n\u003cAnatomy id=\"steps\" /\u003e\n\n```tsx\n\u003cSteps.Root\u003e\n  \u003cSteps.List\u003e\n    \u003cSteps.Item\u003e\n      \u003cSteps.Trigger\u003e\n        \u003cSteps.Indicator /\u003e\n      \u003c/Steps.Trigger\u003e\n      \u003cSteps.Separator /\u003e\n    \u003c/Steps.Item\u003e\n  \u003c/Steps.List\u003e\n  \u003cSteps.Content /\u003e\n  \u003cSteps.CompletedContent /\u003e\n  \u003cSteps.PrevTrigger /\u003e\n  \u003cSteps.NextTrigger /\u003e\n\u003c/Steps.Root\u003e\n```\n\n## Examples\n\n### Basic\n\nHere's a basic example of the `Steps` component.\n\n\u003cExample component=\"steps\" id=\"basic\" /\u003e\n\n### Controlled\n\nUsing the `RootProvider` component, you can control the active step by using the `step` prop and handling the\n`onStepChange` event.\n\n**Example: controlled**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Steps } from '@ark-ui/react/steps'\nimport { useState } from 'react'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/steps.module.css'\n\nconst items = [\n  { value: 'first', title: 'First', description: 'Contact Info' },\n  { value: 'second', title: 'Second', description: 'Date \u0026 Time' },\n  { value: 'third', title: 'Third', description: 'Select Rooms' },\n]\n\nexport const Controlled = () =\u003e {\n  const [step, setStep] = useState(0)\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv className=\"stack\"\u003e\n      \u003coutput\u003ecurrent step: {step + 1}\u003c/output\u003e\n\n      \u003cSteps.Root\n        className={styles.Root}\n        count={items.length}\n        step={step}\n        onStepChange={(details) =\u003e setStep(details.step)}\n      \u003e\n        \u003cSteps.List className={styles.List}\u003e\n          {items.map((item, index) =\u003e (\n            \u003cSteps.Item className={styles.Item} key={index} index={index}\u003e\n              \u003cSteps.Trigger className={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n                \u003cSteps.Indicator className={styles.Indicator}\u003e{index + 1}\u003c/Steps.Indicator\u003e\n                \u003cspan\u003e{item.title}\u003c/span\u003e\n              \u003c/Steps.Trigger\u003e\n              \u003cSteps.Separator className={styles.Separator} /\u003e\n            \u003c/Steps.Item\u003e\n          ))}\n        \u003c/Steps.List\u003e\n\n        {items.map((item, index) =\u003e (\n          \u003cSteps.Content className={styles.Content} key={index} index={index}\u003e\n            {item.title} - {item.description}\n          \u003c/Steps.Content\u003e\n        ))}\n\n        \u003cSteps.CompletedContent className={styles.CompletedContent}\u003e\n          Steps Complete - Thank you for filling out the form!\n        \u003c/Steps.CompletedContent\u003e\n\n        \u003cdiv className={styles.Actions}\u003e\n          \u003cSteps.PrevTrigger className={button.Root}\u003eBack\u003c/Steps.PrevTrigger\u003e\n          \u003cSteps.NextTrigger className={button.Root} data-variant=\"solid\"\u003e\n            Next\n          \u003c/Steps.NextTrigger\u003e\n        \u003c/div\u003e\n      \u003c/Steps.Root\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Steps } from '@ark-ui/solid/steps'\nimport { For, createSignal } from 'solid-js'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/steps.module.css'\n\nconst items = [\n  { value: 'first', title: 'First', description: 'Contact Info' },\n  { value: 'second', title: 'Second', description: 'Date \u0026 Time' },\n  { value: 'third', title: 'Third', description: 'Select Rooms' },\n]\n\nexport const Controlled = () =\u003e {\n  const [step, setStep] = createSignal(0)\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv class=\"stack\"\u003e\n      \u003coutput\u003ecurrent step: {step() + 1}\u003c/output\u003e\n\n      \u003cSteps.Root\n        class={styles.Root}\n        count={items.length}\n        step={step()}\n        onStepChange={(details) =\u003e setStep(details.step)}\n      \u003e\n        \u003cSteps.List class={styles.List}\u003e\n          \u003cFor each={items}\u003e\n            {(item, index) =\u003e (\n              \u003cSteps.Item class={styles.Item} index={index()}\u003e\n                \u003cSteps.Trigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n                  \u003cSteps.Indicator class={styles.Indicator}\u003e{index() + 1}\u003c/Steps.Indicator\u003e\n                  \u003cspan\u003e{item.title}\u003c/span\u003e\n                \u003c/Steps.Trigger\u003e\n                \u003cSteps.Separator class={styles.Separator} /\u003e\n              \u003c/Steps.Item\u003e\n            )}\n          \u003c/For\u003e\n        \u003c/Steps.List\u003e\n\n        \u003cFor each={items}\u003e\n          {(item, index) =\u003e (\n            \u003cSteps.Content class={styles.Content} index={index()}\u003e\n              {item.title} - {item.description}\n            \u003c/Steps.Content\u003e\n          )}\n        \u003c/For\u003e\n\n        \u003cSteps.CompletedContent class={styles.CompletedContent}\u003e\n          Steps Complete - Thank you for filling out the form!\n        \u003c/Steps.CompletedContent\u003e\n\n        \u003cdiv class={styles.Actions}\u003e\n          \u003cSteps.PrevTrigger class={button.Root}\u003eBack\u003c/Steps.PrevTrigger\u003e\n          \u003cSteps.NextTrigger class={button.Root} data-variant=\"solid\"\u003e\n            Next\n          \u003c/Steps.NextTrigger\u003e\n        \u003c/div\u003e\n      \u003c/Steps.Root\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Steps } from '@ark-ui/vue/steps'\nimport { ref } from 'vue'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/steps.module.css'\n\nconst items = [\n  { value: 'first', title: 'First', description: 'Contact Info' },\n  { value: 'second', title: 'Second', description: 'Date \u0026 Time' },\n  { value: 'third', title: 'Third', description: 'Select Rooms' },\n]\n\nconst currentStep = ref(0)\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cdiv class=\"stack\"\u003e\n    \u003coutput\u003ecurrent step: {{ currentStep + 1 }}\u003c/output\u003e\n\n    \u003cSteps.Root v-model:step=\"currentStep\" :class=\"styles.Root\" :count=\"items.length\"\u003e\n      \u003cSteps.List :class=\"styles.List\"\u003e\n        \u003cSteps.Item v-for=\"(item, index) in items\" :key=\"index\" :class=\"styles.Item\" :index=\"index\"\u003e\n          \u003cSteps.Trigger :class=\"styles.Trigger\"\u003e\n            \u003cSteps.Indicator :class=\"styles.Indicator\"\u003e{{ index + 1 }}\u003c/Steps.Indicator\u003e\n            \u003cspan\u003e{{ item.title }}\u003c/span\u003e\n          \u003c/Steps.Trigger\u003e\n          \u003cSteps.Separator :class=\"styles.Separator\" /\u003e\n        \u003c/Steps.Item\u003e\n      \u003c/Steps.List\u003e\n\n      \u003cSteps.Content v-for=\"(item, index) in items\" :key=\"index\" :class=\"styles.Content\" :index=\"index\"\u003e\n        {{ item.title }} - {{ item.description }}\n      \u003c/Steps.Content\u003e\n\n      \u003cSteps.CompletedContent :class=\"styles.CompletedContent\"\u003e\n        Steps Complete - Thank you for filling out the form!\n      \u003c/Steps.CompletedContent\u003e\n\n      \u003cdiv :class=\"styles.Actions\"\u003e\n        \u003cSteps.PrevTrigger :class=\"button.Root\"\u003eBack\u003c/Steps.PrevTrigger\u003e\n        \u003cSteps.NextTrigger :class=\"button.Root\" data-variant=\"solid\"\u003eNext\u003c/Steps.NextTrigger\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n    \u003c/Steps.Root\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Steps } from '@ark-ui/svelte/steps'\n  import button from 'styles/button.module.css'\n  import styles from 'styles/steps.module.css'\n\n  const items = [\n    { value: 'first', title: 'First', description: 'Contact Info' },\n    { value: 'second', title: 'Second', description: 'Date \u0026 Time' },\n    { value: 'third', title: 'Third', description: 'Select Rooms' },\n  ]\n\n  let step = $state(0)\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cdiv class=\"stack\"\u003e\n  \u003coutput\u003ecurrent step: {step + 1}\u003c/output\u003e\n\n  \u003cSteps.Root class={styles.Root} bind:step count={items.length}\u003e\n    \u003cSteps.List class={styles.List}\u003e\n      {#each items as item, index}\n        \u003cSteps.Item class={styles.Item} {index}\u003e\n          \u003cSteps.Trigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n            \u003cSteps.Indicator class={styles.Indicator}\u003e{index + 1}\u003c/Steps.Indicator\u003e\n            \u003cspan\u003e{item.title}\u003c/span\u003e\n          \u003c/Steps.Trigger\u003e\n          \u003cSteps.Separator class={styles.Separator} /\u003e\n        \u003c/Steps.Item\u003e\n      {/each}\n    \u003c/Steps.List\u003e\n\n    {#each items as item, index}\n      \u003cSteps.Content class={styles.Content} {index}\u003e\n        {item.title} - {item.description}\n      \u003c/Steps.Content\u003e\n    {/each}\n\n    \u003cSteps.CompletedContent class={styles.CompletedContent}\u003e\n      Steps Complete - Thank you for filling out the form!\n    \u003c/Steps.CompletedContent\u003e\n\n    \u003cdiv class={styles.Actions}\u003e\n      \u003cSteps.PrevTrigger class={button.Root}\u003eBack\u003c/Steps.PrevTrigger\u003e\n      \u003cSteps.NextTrigger class={button.Root} data-variant=\"solid\"\u003eNext\u003c/Steps.NextTrigger\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  \u003c/Steps.Root\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Root Provider\n\nAn alternative way to control the steps is to use the `RootProvider` component and the `useSteps` hook. This way you can\naccess the state and methods from outside the component.\n\n**Example: root-provider**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Steps, useSteps } from '@ark-ui/react/steps'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/steps.module.css'\n\nconst items = [\n  { value: 'first', title: 'First', description: 'Contact Info' },\n  { value: 'second', title: 'Second', description: 'Date \u0026 Time' },\n  { value: 'third', title: 'Third', description: 'Select Rooms' },\n]\n\nexport const RootProvider = () =\u003e {\n  const steps = useSteps({ count: items.length })\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv className=\"stack\"\u003e\n      \u003coutput\u003ecurrent step: {steps.value + 1}\u003c/output\u003e\n\n      \u003cSteps.RootProvider className={styles.Root} value={steps}\u003e\n        \u003cSteps.List className={styles.List}\u003e\n          {items.map((item, index) =\u003e (\n            \u003cSteps.Item className={styles.Item} key={index} index={index}\u003e\n              \u003cSteps.Trigger className={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n                \u003cSteps.Indicator className={styles.Indicator}\u003e{index + 1}\u003c/Steps.Indicator\u003e\n                \u003cspan\u003e{item.title}\u003c/span\u003e\n              \u003c/Steps.Trigger\u003e\n              \u003cSteps.Separator className={styles.Separator} /\u003e\n            \u003c/Steps.Item\u003e\n          ))}\n        \u003c/Steps.List\u003e\n\n        {items.map((item, index) =\u003e (\n          \u003cSteps.Content className={styles.Content} key={index} index={index}\u003e\n            {item.title} - {item.description}\n          \u003c/Steps.Content\u003e\n        ))}\n\n        \u003cSteps.CompletedContent className={styles.CompletedContent}\u003e\n          Steps Complete - Thank you for filling out the form!\n        \u003c/Steps.CompletedContent\u003e\n\n        \u003cdiv className={styles.Actions}\u003e\n          \u003cSteps.PrevTrigger className={button.Root}\u003eBack\u003c/Steps.PrevTrigger\u003e\n          \u003cSteps.NextTrigger className={button.Root} data-variant=\"solid\"\u003e\n            Next\n          \u003c/Steps.NextTrigger\u003e\n        \u003c/div\u003e\n      \u003c/Steps.RootProvider\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Steps, useSteps } from '@ark-ui/solid/steps'\nimport { For } from 'solid-js'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/steps.module.css'\n\nconst items = [\n  { value: 'first', title: 'First', description: 'Contact Info' },\n  { value: 'second', title: 'Second', description: 'Date \u0026 Time' },\n  { value: 'third', title: 'Third', description: 'Select Rooms' },\n]\n\nexport const RootProvider = () =\u003e {\n  const steps = useSteps({ count: items.length })\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv class=\"stack\"\u003e\n      \u003coutput\u003ecurrent step: {steps().value + 1}\u003c/output\u003e\n\n      \u003cSteps.RootProvider class={styles.Root} value={steps}\u003e\n        \u003cSteps.List class={styles.List}\u003e\n          \u003cFor each={items}\u003e\n            {(item, index) =\u003e (\n              \u003cSteps.Item class={styles.Item} index={index()}\u003e\n                \u003cSteps.Trigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n                  \u003cSteps.Indicator class={styles.Indicator}\u003e{index() + 1}\u003c/Steps.Indicator\u003e\n                  \u003cspan\u003e{item.title}\u003c/span\u003e\n                \u003c/Steps.Trigger\u003e\n                \u003cSteps.Separator class={styles.Separator} /\u003e\n              \u003c/Steps.Item\u003e\n            )}\n          \u003c/For\u003e\n        \u003c/Steps.List\u003e\n\n        \u003cFor each={items}\u003e\n          {(item, index) =\u003e (\n            \u003cSteps.Content class={styles.Content} index={index()}\u003e\n              {item.title} - {item.description}\n            \u003c/Steps.Content\u003e\n          )}\n        \u003c/For\u003e\n\n        \u003cSteps.CompletedContent class={styles.CompletedContent}\u003e\n          Steps Complete - Thank you for filling out the form!\n        \u003c/Steps.CompletedContent\u003e\n\n        \u003cdiv class={styles.Actions}\u003e\n          \u003cSteps.PrevTrigger class={button.Root}\u003eBack\u003c/Steps.PrevTrigger\u003e\n          \u003cSteps.NextTrigger class={button.Root} data-variant=\"solid\"\u003e\n            Next\n          \u003c/Steps.NextTrigger\u003e\n        \u003c/div\u003e\n      \u003c/Steps.RootProvider\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Steps, useSteps } from '@ark-ui/vue/steps'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/steps.module.css'\n\nconst items = [\n  { value: 'first', title: 'First', description: 'Contact Info' },\n  { value: 'second', title: 'Second', description: 'Date \u0026 Time' },\n  { value: 'third', title: 'Third', description: 'Select Rooms' },\n]\n\nconst steps = useSteps({ count: items.length })\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cdiv class=\"stack\"\u003e\n    \u003coutput\u003ecurrent step: {{ steps.value + 1 }}\u003c/output\u003e\n\n    \u003cSteps.RootProvider :class=\"styles.Root\" :value=\"steps\"\u003e\n      \u003cSteps.List :class=\"styles.List\"\u003e\n        \u003cSteps.Item v-for=\"(item, index) in items\" :key=\"index\" :class=\"styles.Item\" :index=\"index\"\u003e\n          \u003cSteps.Trigger :class=\"styles.Trigger\"\u003e\n            \u003cSteps.Indicator :class=\"styles.Indicator\"\u003e{{ index + 1 }}\u003c/Steps.Indicator\u003e\n            \u003cspan\u003e{{ item.title }}\u003c/span\u003e\n          \u003c/Steps.Trigger\u003e\n          \u003cSteps.Separator :class=\"styles.Separator\" /\u003e\n        \u003c/Steps.Item\u003e\n      \u003c/Steps.List\u003e\n\n      \u003cSteps.Content v-for=\"(item, index) in items\" :key=\"index\" :class=\"styles.Content\" :index=\"index\"\u003e\n        {{ item.title }} - {{ item.description }}\n      \u003c/Steps.Content\u003e\n\n      \u003cSteps.CompletedContent :class=\"styles.CompletedContent\"\u003e\n        Steps Complete - Thank you for filling out the form!\n      \u003c/Steps.CompletedContent\u003e\n\n      \u003cdiv :class=\"styles.Actions\"\u003e\n        \u003cSteps.PrevTrigger :class=\"button.Root\"\u003eBack\u003c/Steps.PrevTrigger\u003e\n        \u003cSteps.NextTrigger :class=\"button.Root\" data-variant=\"solid\"\u003eNext\u003c/Steps.NextTrigger\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n    \u003c/Steps.RootProvider\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Steps, useSteps } from '@ark-ui/svelte/steps'\n  import button from 'styles/button.module.css'\n  import styles from 'styles/steps.module.css'\n\n  const items = [\n    { value: 'first', title: 'First', description: 'Contact Info' },\n    { value: 'second', title: 'Second', description: 'Date \u0026 Time' },\n    { value: 'third', title: 'Third', description: 'Select Rooms' },\n  ]\n\n  const id = $props.id()\n  const steps = useSteps({ id, count: items.length })\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cdiv class=\"stack\"\u003e\n  \u003coutput\u003ecurrent step: {steps().value + 1}\u003c/output\u003e\n\n  \u003cSteps.RootProvider class={styles.Root} value={steps}\u003e\n    \u003cSteps.List class={styles.List}\u003e\n      {#each items as item, index}\n        \u003cSteps.Item class={styles.Item} {index}\u003e\n          \u003cSteps.Trigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n            \u003cSteps.Indicator class={styles.Indicator}\u003e{index + 1}\u003c/Steps.Indicator\u003e\n            \u003cspan\u003e{item.title}\u003c/span\u003e\n          \u003c/Steps.Trigger\u003e\n          \u003cSteps.Separator class={styles.Separator} /\u003e\n        \u003c/Steps.Item\u003e\n      {/each}\n    \u003c/Steps.List\u003e\n\n    {#each items as item, index}\n      \u003cSteps.Content class={styles.Content} {index}\u003e\n        {item.title} - {item.description}\n      \u003c/Steps.Content\u003e\n    {/each}\n\n    \u003cSteps.CompletedContent class={styles.CompletedContent}\u003e\n      Steps Complete - Thank you for filling out the form!\n    \u003c/Steps.CompletedContent\u003e\n\n    \u003cdiv class={styles.Actions}\u003e\n      \u003cSteps.PrevTrigger class={button.Root}\u003eBack\u003c/Steps.PrevTrigger\u003e\n      \u003cSteps.NextTrigger class={button.Root} data-variant=\"solid\"\u003eNext\u003c/Steps.NextTrigger\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  \u003c/Steps.RootProvider\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Vertical\n\nUse the `orientation` prop to display the steps vertically.\n\n**Example: vertical**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Steps } from '@ark-ui/react/steps'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/steps.module.css'\n\nconst items = [\n  { value: 'first', title: 'First', description: 'Contact Info' },\n  { value: 'second', title: 'Second', description: 'Date \u0026 Time' },\n  { value: 'third', title: 'Third', description: 'Select Rooms' },\n]\n\nexport const Vertical = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cSteps.Root className={styles.Root} count={items.length} orientation=\"vertical\"\u003e\n      \u003cSteps.List className={styles.List}\u003e\n        {items.map((item, index) =\u003e (\n          \u003cSteps.Item className={styles.Item} key={index} index={index}\u003e\n            \u003cSteps.Trigger className={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n              \u003cSteps.Indicator className={styles.Indicator}\u003e{index + 1}\u003c/Steps.Indicator\u003e\n              \u003cspan\u003e{item.title}\u003c/span\u003e\n            \u003c/Steps.Trigger\u003e\n            \u003cSteps.Separator className={styles.Separator} /\u003e\n          \u003c/Steps.Item\u003e\n        ))}\n      \u003c/Steps.List\u003e\n\n      {items.map((item, index) =\u003e (\n        \u003cSteps.Content className={styles.Content} key={index} index={index}\u003e\n          \u003cdiv className=\"vstack\"\u003e\n            \u003cspan\u003e\n              {item.title} - {item.description}\n            \u003c/span\u003e\n            \u003cdiv className={styles.Actions}\u003e\n              \u003cSteps.PrevTrigger className={button.Root}\u003eBack\u003c/Steps.PrevTrigger\u003e\n              \u003cSteps.NextTrigger className={button.Root} data-variant=\"solid\"\u003e\n                Next\n              \u003c/Steps.NextTrigger\u003e\n            \u003c/div\u003e\n          \u003c/div\u003e\n        \u003c/Steps.Content\u003e\n      ))}\n\n      \u003cSteps.CompletedContent className={styles.CompletedContent}\u003e\n        \u003cdiv className=\"vstack\"\u003e\n          \u003cspan\u003eSteps Complete - Thank you for filling out the form!\u003c/span\u003e\n          \u003cSteps.PrevTrigger className={button.Root}\u003eBack\u003c/Steps.PrevTrigger\u003e\n        \u003c/div\u003e\n      \u003c/Steps.CompletedContent\u003e\n    \u003c/Steps.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Steps } from '@ark-ui/solid/steps'\nimport { For } from 'solid-js'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/steps.module.css'\n\nconst items = [\n  { value: 'first', title: 'First', description: 'Contact Info' },\n  { value: 'second', title: 'Second', description: 'Date \u0026 Time' },\n  { value: 'third', title: 'Third', description: 'Select Rooms' },\n]\n\nexport const Vertical = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cSteps.Root class={styles.Root} count={items.length} orientation=\"vertical\"\u003e\n      \u003cSteps.List class={styles.List}\u003e\n        \u003cFor each={items}\u003e\n          {(item, index) =\u003e (\n            \u003cSteps.Item class={styles.Item} index={index()}\u003e\n              \u003cSteps.Trigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n                \u003cSteps.Indicator class={styles.Indicator}\u003e{index() + 1}\u003c/Steps.Indicator\u003e\n                \u003cspan\u003e{item.title}\u003c/span\u003e\n              \u003c/Steps.Trigger\u003e\n              \u003cSteps.Separator class={styles.Separator} /\u003e\n            \u003c/Steps.Item\u003e\n          )}\n        \u003c/For\u003e\n      \u003c/Steps.List\u003e\n\n      \u003cFor each={items}\u003e\n        {(item, index) =\u003e (\n          \u003cSteps.Content class={styles.Content} index={index()}\u003e\n            \u003cdiv class=\"vstack\"\u003e\n              \u003cspan\u003e\n                {item.title} - {item.description}\n              \u003c/span\u003e\n              \u003cdiv class={styles.Actions}\u003e\n                \u003cSteps.PrevTrigger class={button.Root}\u003eBack\u003c/Steps.PrevTrigger\u003e\n                \u003cSteps.NextTrigger class={button.Root} data-variant=\"solid\"\u003e\n                  Next\n                \u003c/Steps.NextTrigger\u003e\n              \u003c/div\u003e\n            \u003c/div\u003e\n          \u003c/Steps.Content\u003e\n        )}\n      \u003c/For\u003e\n\n      \u003cSteps.CompletedContent class={styles.CompletedContent}\u003e\n        \u003cdiv class=\"vstack\"\u003e\n          \u003cspan\u003eSteps Complete - Thank you for filling out the form!\u003c/span\u003e\n          \u003cSteps.PrevTrigger class={button.Root}\u003eBack\u003c/Steps.PrevTrigger\u003e\n        \u003c/div\u003e\n      \u003c/Steps.CompletedContent\u003e\n    \u003c/Steps.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Steps } from '@ark-ui/vue/steps'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/steps.module.css'\n\nconst items = [\n  { value: 'first', title: 'First', description: 'Contact Info' },\n  { value: 'second', title: 'Second', description: 'Date \u0026 Time' },\n  { value: 'third', title: 'Third', description: 'Select Rooms' },\n]\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cSteps.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" :count=\"items.length\" orientation=\"vertical\"\u003e\n    \u003cSteps.List }}\u003c/span\u003e\n        \u003c/Steps.Trigger\u003e\n        \u003cSteps.Separator :class=\"styles.Separator\" /\u003e\n      \u003c/Steps.Item\u003e\n    \u003c/Steps.List\u003e\n\n    \u003cSteps.Content v-for=\"(item, index) in items\" :key=\"index\" :class=\"styles.Content\" :index=\"index\"\u003e\n      \u003cdiv class=\"vstack\"\u003e\n        \u003cspan\u003e{{ item.title }} - \u003cSteps.CompletedContent :class=\"styles.CompletedContent\"\u003e\n      \u003cdiv class=\"vstack\"\u003e\n        \u003cspan\u003eSteps Complete - Thank you for filling out the form!\u003c/span\u003e\n        \u003cSteps.PrevTrigger :class=\"button.Root\"\u003eBack\u003c/Steps.PrevTrigger\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n    \u003c/Steps.CompletedContent\u003e\n  \u003c/Steps.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Steps } from '@ark-ui/svelte/steps'\n  import button from 'styles/button.module.css'\n  import styles from 'styles/steps.module.css'\n\n  const items = [\n    { value: 'first', title: 'First', description: 'Contact Info' },\n    { value: 'second', title: 'Second', description: 'Date \u0026 Time' },\n    { value: 'third', title: 'Third', description: 'Select Rooms' },\n  ]\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cSteps.Root class={styles.Root} count={items.length} orientation=\"vertical\"\u003e\n  \u003cSteps.List class={styles.List}\u003e\n    {#each items as item, index}\n      \u003cSteps.Item class={styles.Item} {index}\u003e\n        \u003cSteps.Trigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n          \u003cSteps.Indicator class={styles.Indicator}\u003e{index + 1}\u003c/Steps.Indicator\u003e\n          \u003cspan\u003e{item.title}\u003c/span\u003e\n        \u003c/Steps.Trigger\u003e\n        \u003cSteps.Separator class={styles.Separator} /\u003e\n      \u003c/Steps.Item\u003e\n    {/each}\n  \u003c/Steps.List\u003e\n\n  {#each items as item, index}\n    \u003cSteps.Content class={styles.Content} {index}\u003e\n      \u003cdiv class=\"vstack\"\u003e\n        \u003cspan\u003e{item.title} - {item.description}\u003c/span\u003e\n        \u003cdiv class={styles.Actions}\u003e\n          \u003cSteps.PrevTrigger class={button.Root}\u003eBack\u003c/Steps.PrevTrigger\u003e\n \u003c/Steps.CompletedContent\u003e\n\u003c/Steps.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n## API Reference\n\n### Props\n\n**Component API Reference**\n\n#### React\n\n**Root Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `asChild` | `boolean` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n| `count` | `number` | No | The total number of steps |\n| `defaultStep` | `number` | No | The initial value of the stepper when rendered.\nUse when you don't need to control the value of the stepper. |\n| `ids` | `ElementIds` | No | The custom ids for the stepper elements |\n| `isStepSkippable` | `(index: number) =\u003e boolean` | No | Whether a step can be skipped during navigation.\nSkippable steps are bypassed when using next/prev. |\n| `isStepValid` | `(index: number) =\u003e boolean` | No | Whether a step is valid. Invalid steps block forward navigation in linear mode. |\n| `linear` | `boolean` | No | If `true`, the stepper requires the user to complete the steps in order |\n| `onStepChange` | `(details: StepChangeDetails) =\u003e void` | No | Callback to be called when the value changes |\n| `onStepComplete` | `VoidFunction` | No | Callback to be called when a step is completed |\n| `onStepInvalid` | `(details: StepInvalidDetails) =\u003e void` | No | Called when navigation is blocked due to an invalid step. |\n| `orientation` | `'horizontal' | 'vertical'` | No | The orientation of the stepper |\n| `step` | `number` | No | The controlled value of the stepper |\n\n\n**Root Data Attributes:**\n\n| Attribute | Value |\n|-----------|-------|\n| `[data-scope]` | steps |\n| `[data-part]` | root |\n| `[data-orientation]` | The orientation of the steps |\n\n\n**Root CSS Variables:**\n\n| Variable | Description |\n|----------|-------------|\n| `--percent` | The percent value for the Root |\n\n\n**CompletedContent Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `asChild` | `boolean` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n\n\n**Content Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `index` | `number` | Yes |  |\n| `asChild` | `boolean` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n\n\n**Content Data Attributes:**\n\n| Attribute | Value |\n|-----------|-------|\n| `[data-scope]` | steps |\n| `[data-part]` | content |\n| `[data-state]` | \"open\" | \"closed\" |\n| `[data-orientation]` | The orientation of the content |\n\n\n**Indicator Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `asChild` | `boolean` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n\n\n**Indicator Data Attributes:**\n\n| Attribute | Value |\n|-----------|-------|\n| `[data-scope]` | steps |\n| `[data-part]` | indicator |\n| `[data-complete]` | Present when the indicator value is complete |\n| `[data-current]` | Present when current |\n| `[data-incomplete]` |  |\n\n\n**Item Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `index` | `number` | Yes |  |\n| `asChild` | `boolean` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n\n\n**Item Data Attributes:**\n\n| Attribute | Value |\n|-----------|-------|\n| `[data-scope]` | steps |\n| `[data-part]` | item |\n| `[data-orientation]` | The orientation of the item |\n| `[data-skippable]` |  |\n\n\n**List Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `asChild` | `boolean` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n\n\n**List Data Attributes:**\n\n| Attribute | Value |\n|-----------|-------|\n| `[data-scope]` | steps |\n| `[data-part]` | list |\n| `[data-orientation]` | The orientation of the list |\n\n\n**NextTrigger Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `asChild` | `boolean` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n\n\n**PrevTrigger Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `asChild` | `boolean` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n\n\n**Progress Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `asChild` | `boolean` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n\n\n**Progress Data Attributes:**\n\n| Attribute | Value |\n|-----------|-------|\n| `[data-scope]` | steps |\n| `[data-part]` | progress |\n| `[data-complete]` | Present when the progress value is complete |\n\n\n**RootProvider Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `value` | `UseStepsReturn` | Yes |  |\n| `asChild` | `boolean` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n\n\n**Separator Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `asChild` | `boolean` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n\n\n**Separator Data Attributes:**\n\n| Attribute | Value |\n|-----------|-------|\n| `[data-scope]` | steps |\n| `[data-part]` | separator |\n| `[data-orientation]` | The orientation of the separator |\n| `[data-complete]` | Present when the separator value is complete |\n| `[data-current]` | Present when current |\n| `[data-incomplete]` |  |\n\n\n**Trigger Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `asChild` | `boolean` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n\n\n**Trigger Data Attributes:**\n\n| Attribute | Value |\n|-----------|-------|\n| `[data-scope]` | steps |\n| `[data-part]` | trigger |\n| `[data-state]` | \"open\" | \"closed\" |\n| `[data-orientation]` | The orientation of the trigger |\n| `[data-complete]` | Present when the trigger value is complete |\n| `[data-current]` | Present when current |\n| `[data-incomplete]` |  |\n\n\n#### Solid\n\n**Root Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `asChild` | `(props: ParentProps\u003c'div'\u003e) =\u003e Element` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n| `count` | `number` | No | The total number of steps |\n| `defaultStep` | `number` | No | The initial value of the stepper when rendered.\nUse when you don't need to control the value of the stepper. |\n| `ids` | `ElementIds` | No | The custom ids for the stepper elements |\n| `isStepSkippable` | `(index: number) =\u003e boolean` | No | Whether a step can be skipped during navigation.\nSkippable steps are bypassed when using next/prev. |\n| `isStepValid` | `(index: number) =\u003e boolean` | No | Whether a step is valid. Invalid steps block forward navigation in linear mode. |\n| `linear` | `boolean` | No | If `true`, the stepper requires the user to complete the steps in order |\n| `onStepChange` | `(details: StepChangeDetails) =\u003e void` | No | Callback to be called when the value changes |\n| `onStepComplete` | `VoidFunction` | No | Callback to be called when a step is completed |\n| `onStepInvalid` | `(details: StepInvalidDetails) =\u003e void` | No | Called when navigation is blocked due to an invalid step. |\n| `orientation` | `'horizontal' | 'vertical'` | No | The orientation of the stepper |\n| `step` | `number` | No | The controlled value of the stepper |\n\n\n**Root Data Attributes:**\n\n| Attribute | Value |\n|-----------|-------|\n| `[data-scope]` | steps |\n| `[data-part]` | root |\n| `[data-orientation]` | The orientation of the steps |\n\n\n**Root CSS Variables:**\n\n| Variable | Description |\n|----------|-------------|\n| `--percent` | The percent value for the Root |\n\n\n**CompletedContent Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `asChild` | `(props: ParentProps\u003c'div'\u003e) =\u003e Element` | No |
